***услуга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́га</a> (2189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslúga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>service, favour, good turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">okázyvatʹ komú-libo uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do smb. a service; to do smb. a good turn</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плоху́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">okázyvatʹ komú-libo ploxúju uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do smb. an ill turn</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платить.html>плати́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">platítʹ uslúgoj za uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предлагать.html>предлага́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">predlagátʹ svoí uslúgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come forward, to offer one's services</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dóbryje uslúgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">good offices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плоха́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ploxája uslúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ill turn, injury</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uslúga za uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one good turn deserves another</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k vášim uslúgam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at your service</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>plural</i> services, attendance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коммунальный.html>коммуна́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kommunálʹnyje uslúgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">public utilities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sféra uslúg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">human services, non-manufacturing business, service</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:услышать.html>услы́шать</a> (470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услышать.html>услы́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslýšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smell, to feel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:услышать.html>услы́шал</a></b> како́й-то <a href = vnd.unilang:странный.html>стра́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>запах</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>uslýšal</b> kakój-to stránnyj zapax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I smelled something strange./I felt some strange smell.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***усматривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усматривать.html>усма́тривать</a> (25181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усматривать.html>усма́тривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usmátrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to see <i>(in)</i>, to perceive <i>(in)</i>, to discover <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усматривать.html>усма́триваю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плохо́го</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja ne <b>usmátrivaju</b> v étom ničevó ploxóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't see anything wrong in this; there is nothing wrong with this</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look <i>(after)</i>, to attend <i>(to)</i>, to keep an eye <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a> (14723)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usmotrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усматривать.html>усма́тривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to see <i>(in)</i>, to perceive <i>(in)</i>, to discover <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usmotrétʹ</b> obídu v predložénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feel slighted/offended by the suggestion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:непристойность.html>непристо́йность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неви́нном <a href = vnd.unilang:стихотворение.html>стихотворе́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>usmotréli</b> nepristójnostʹ v nevínnom stixotvorénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they found/discovered an obscenity in an innocent poem</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look <i>(after)</i>, to attend <i>(to)</i>, to keep an eye <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмо́тришь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za vsem ne <b>usmótrišʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"> one can't be in two places at once</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***уснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уснуть.html>усну́ть</a> (2747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*usъnǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall asleep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*u-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъpati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sleep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swep-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-усопш-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усохнуть.html>усо́хнуть</a> (21916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сохнуть.html>со́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sóxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усохнуть.html>усо́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usóxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усыха́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shrivel, to wither, becoming hard</li>
<li>to dry up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shrink <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as a result of drying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to shrivel up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from old age</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uspétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успевать.html>успева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uspevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to have time, to find time, to manage, to succeed</li>
<li>to arrive in time (for), to be in time (for)</li>
<li>to catch (a train, bus)</li>
<li>to get on well, to make progress, to advance <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in one's studies</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to keep pace <i>with someone</i></li></ol>

***успеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a> (317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spewd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">press, hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">speed</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uspétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успевать.html>успева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to have time, to find time</li>
<li>to manage (to do something), to succeed</li>
<li>to arrive in time (for), to be in time (for)</li>
<li>to catch (a train, bus)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>One of the notable ways to use the verb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></b> is to indicate two events happening subsequently in a sudden way. The main clause includes <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ла</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ло</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ли</a></b> and the subordinate clause starts with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></b>. For example:
</p>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завершить.html>заверши́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тере</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:энергосистема.html>энергосисте́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ния</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ne uspél</b> on zaveršítʹ svojú rabótu na kompʹjútɛre, <b>kak</b> slučílasʹ avárija v enɛrgosistéme zdánija.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i><b>Just as</b> he (almost) finished his work on a computer, a blackout occurred in the building.</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>The main clause has an additional perfective infinitive verb due to the finite verb, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a></b>, also being perfective. Thus, the main clause evokes an action that intends to reach completion, but is suddenly interrupted with another event (as described by the main clause). Thus, the two subsequent events may be slightly overlapped with each other or lack any interval.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успешный.html>успе́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uspéšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uspétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to catch, to make it</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to ripen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spewd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">press, hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">speed</i>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успех.html>успе́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uspéx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успешный.html>успе́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uspéšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)успе́шнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)успе́шней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успешный.html>успе́шный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>successful <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">resulting in success</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
